    Class Citizenship Read the statement below from the Syllabus before answering any of the questions. You are expected to be totally honest with your answers to the questions. Class Citizenship (5%). You are expected to arrive to class on time, come prepared and participate. Anything less than this will directly affect your semester grade. Punctuality. Students walking in late to class or leaving early is one of the rudest offenses that can be done in the classroom. You are considered to be tardy if you arrive once the opening prayer has been said. Each tardy or early leave from class will affect your semester grade negatively. Participation. There are several aspects to Participation: Beginning of Class Report. At the beginning of each class we will have a brief report from students (called upon randomly) about their reading for the day or Learning Capture. You are expected to be ready when called upon. Class Discussion. You are expected to come prepared to class so that you may actively participate in class activities such as asking questions, volunteering answers, and so on. Your level on participation will directly affect your semester grade. Rules of Conduct. Please be respectful of others around you. Disturbing in class will affect your standing in class and your grade. Violation of any of the following class rules will result in a lower final semester grade. Repeat violations of one or a combination of these rules will result in you no longer being welcome in class. Consider this to be your final warning: NO CELL PHONES, LAPTOPS, TABLETS, OR ANY OTHER ELECTRONIC DEVICES ARE TO BE USED DURING CLASS UNLESS DIRECTED BY THE INSTRUCTOR (turn off vibration and sound modes and put away in your bag), No food or drink (water only), No disrupting or causing distractions (such as visiting or doing homework for another class, being chronically late to class, sleeping, etc.), No Honor Code infractions (such as male students failing to attend class clean shaven).
